Eating disorder omissions I love the show but Iâ€™m in awe of how there is so much discussion of embodiment and eating disorder recovery without any awareness of fatphobia and diet culture. The last episode in embodiment literally lists all oppressions but never fatness. The show is otherwise so political about queerness and gender and feminism, but the silence around body size is glaring. You canâ€™t discuss eating disorders in a serious way without the context that we live in a world that hates fat people, especially women, and is set up against fatness. Eating disorders can be about a lot of things - control, trauma ,misogyny - as this show is so eloquent about. But eating disorders would not exist the way they do without this crucial cultural context that we are taught that fat is a personal failure from before we can even talk.  Bodies come in all sizes due to genetics and always have, and all bodies are good bodies. You cannot tell how healthy someone is by looking at them. A show that so often talks about ED and trauma should acknowledge this.

Every state has different laws on this. The primary decides the candidate on the state ballots, not the convention. State laws control how, and even if, a candidate can be replaced after the primary.
